In my room, my clothes and psychology are very relaxed and safe, but the door of the room was opened directly by the male waiter by swiping his card from the outside! This is obviously a problem of negligence in management and lack of personnel training, but the hotel is explaining that "he has been knocking on the door for a long time, so he opened the door because he thought there was no one inside." May I ask if I can't hear the door knocking in the shower, can he assume that there is no one in the room and can swipe his card to come in? For every room in the hotel, has the guest swiped his card to check in? Can the hotel not see the status?

The manager apologized repeatedly and gave me dinner coupons. In order to stop her apologizing, I accepted it, but any compensation was meaningless to me. I didn't sleep all night and I couldn't think of any reason to calm down.
That's it, Ramada is not short of me as a guest.
